  export class $my_bug_db extends $mol_object2 {

    @ $mol_mem
    db() {
      return {
        msg: 'i am db',
        query: () => new Promise(r => r(`hello from db.query`))
      }
    }
    
    @ $mol_fiber.method
    query() {
      const db = this.db()
      const func = $mol_fiber_sync( () => db.query() )
      const res = func()
      console.log(`${this}.query()`, res)
      return res
    }
    
    @ $mol_fiber.method
    get() {
      const res = this.query()
      console.log( `${this}.get()` , res )
      return res
    }
    
  }

  export class $my_bug extends $mol_server {
    
    @ $mol_mem
    db() {
      return new $my_bug_db
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    watch( next?: Map<'client', Set<string>> ) {
      return next ?? new Map
    }
    
    @ $mol_fiber.method
    get() {
      console.log(`${this}.get():1`)

      // Block 1 
      // if ( !this.watch().get( 'client' ) ) {
      //   this.watch().set( 'client' , new Set )
      // }
      // this.watch().get( 'client' ).add( 'key' )
      
      // Block 2
      const watch = this.watch()
      if (!watch.get('client')) {
        watch.set('client', new Set)
      }
      watch.get('client').add('key')
      
      const res = this.db().get() // undefined when block1
      console.log(`${this}.get():2` , res)
    }
    
  }
  
  export function $my_bug_bootstrap() {
    const inst = new $my_bug
    inst.get()
  }
  
  $mol_fiber_root( $my_bug_bootstrap )()

}

namespace $.$$ {

  export class $my_timer extends $.$my_timer {
    
    @ $mol_mem
    timer( next? : any ) {
      return next
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    time( next? : string ) {
      return next ?? 'Disabled'
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    loop( start : boolean ) {
      if ( !start ) {
        return clearInterval( this.timer() )
      }
      
      const timer = setInterval( () => this.time( new Date().toISOString() ) , 1000 )
      this.timer( timer )

    }
    
    start() {
      this.loop( true )
    }
    
    stop() {
      this.loop( false )
    }

  }

    @ $mol_mem
